φιμός
φῑμόω, fut. -ώσω <br><b>to muzzle, shut up as with a muzzle</b>, φ. τῷ ξύλῳ τὸν αὐχένα <b>to make fast</b> his neck in the pillory, Ar.: metaph. <b>to muzzle, put to silence</b>, NTest.: Pass., aor1 imperat.  φιμώθητι <b>be thou silenced</b>, id=NTest.
